+## ‚úÖ **ISSUE RESOLVED** - Bug Fixed and Tested
 
+**Original Problem**: 
+In LOCAL_BUILD_MODE, when loading a first song (Song 1), the application correctly:
+- Loads and displays the waveform
+- Analyzes and displays BPM (e.g., 101.0)
+- Analyzes and displays Key (e.g., 9A E minor) 
+- Displays the track title correctly
+
+However, when loading a second song (Song 2) by drag-and-drop to replace the first song:
+- The waveform updates correctly to show Song 2
+- The BPM field does NOT update (still shows Song 1's BPM)
+- The Key field does NOT update (still shows Song 1's Key)
+- The track title does NOT update (still shows Song 1's title)
 
 **Desired Behavior**: 
-The program
-License Key: 
+When any new song is loaded (whether first song or replacement song), ALL UI fields should update correctly:
+- Waveform should display the new song's waveform ‚úì (working)
+- BPM field should show the new song's analyzed BPM
+- Key field should show the new song's analyzed key
+- Track title should show the new song's title
+- All fields should be consistent and reflect the currently loaded song
+
+**Error Evidence**:
+From the logs, when Song 2 loads, there's a critical error:
+```
+C7_GUI_Z_AsyncManager - ERROR - [AsyncManager] BPM/Key worker is not set up. Call setup_bpm_key_worker() first.
+```
+
+This suggests the BPM/Key analysis worker is not properly initialized for subsequent song loads.
+
+## üîß **RESOLUTION SUMMARY**
+
+**Root Cause Found**: Two critical bugs in the async analysis workflow:
+1. **AsyncManager Worker Destruction**: After first song analysis, `_handle_thread_finished()` called `deleteLater()` on worker/thread, destroying them for subsequent songs
+2. **Missing State Reset Signal**: Drag-and-drop file loading bypassed the `state_reset_for_new_file` signal emission
+
+**Fixes Applied**:
+- **Stage 1**: Modified `AsyncManager._handle_thread_finished()` to keep workers alive for reuse
+- **Stage 2**: Added state reset signal emission to `WaveformWidget._handle_dropped_files()`
+
+**Testing Verified**: Three-song test confirms BPM/Key/Title now update correctly for all subsequent song loads
+

+# Song Loading UI Update Bug: Research & Analysis
+
+## Restated Feature/Problem
+In LOCAL_BUILD_MODE, when loading a first song, all UI components update correctly (waveform, BPM, Key, Title). However, when loading a second song via drag-and-drop to replace the first song, only the waveform updates while the BPM, Key, and Title fields remain stuck showing the first song's values. This creates an inconsistent UI state where the displayed analysis data doesn't match the currently loaded audio.
+
+**Critical Error Evidence:**
+```
+C7_GUI_Z_AsyncManager - ERROR - [AsyncManager] BPM/Key worker is not set up. Call setup_bpm_key_worker() first.
+```
+
+## Root Cause Analysis
+
+### 1. **AsyncManager Worker Lifecycle Bug**
+The core issue is in `C7_GUI_Z_AsyncManager.py`, specifically in the `_handle_thread_finished()` method:
+
+```python:113-123:C7_GUI_Z_AsyncManager.py
+def _handle_thread_finished(self):
+    """Internal handler for when the thread has finished."""
+    self.logger.info("[AsyncManager] Analysis QThread finished.")
+    # Clean up references
+    if self.bpm_key_thread:
+        self.bpm_key_thread.deleteLater()
+        self.bmp_key_thread = None  # BUG: This should be self.bpm_key_thread = None
+    if self.bpm_key_worker:
+        self.bpm_key_worker.deleteLater()
+        self.bmp_key_worker = None  # BUG: This should be self.bmp_key_worker = None
+```
+
+**Problem:** After the first song's analysis completes, the worker and thread are deleted and set to `None`, but they are never recreated for subsequent analyses.
+
+### 2. **Worker Setup Only Happens Once**
+Looking at `C7_GUI_1_AppController.py` lines 152-158:
+
+```python:152-158:C7_GUI_1_AppController.py
+# --- Initialize AsyncManager for BPM/Key Analysis ---
+self.async_manager = AsyncManager(parent=self)
+self.async_manager.setup_bmp_key_worker(
+    detect_bmp_func=self.detect_bpm_func,
+    analyze_key_func=self.analyze_key_func
+)
+```
+
+The `setup_bpm_key_worker()` is called **only once** during app initialization, not after each analysis completes.
+
+### 3. **File Loading Flow Analysis**
+
+**For First Song (Working):**
+1. User drags Song 1 ‚Üí `WaveformDragDropHandler.dropEvent()` 
+2. ‚Üí `WaveformWidget._handle_dropped_files()` 
+3. ‚Üí `FileStateManager.finalize_file_load(True)` 
+4. ‚Üí `AsyncManager.start_analysis()` ‚úì (worker exists)
+5. ‚Üí BPM/Key analysis runs successfully 
+6. ‚Üí Results propagated to UI ‚úì
+7. ‚Üí `AsyncManager._handle_worker_completion()` ‚Üí `_shutdown_thread()` 
+8. ‚Üí `_handle_thread_finished()` ‚Üí **Worker deleted!** ‚ùå
+
+**For Second Song (Broken):**
+1. User drags Song 2 ‚Üí Same flow as above through step 3
+2. ‚Üí `AsyncManager.start_analysis()` ‚ùå **Worker is None!**
+3. ‚Üí Error: "BPM/Key worker is not set up" 
+4. ‚Üí No analysis runs ‚Üí No UI updates for BPM/Key/Title
+
+### 4. **Code References Supporting This Analysis**
+
+**Drag-Drop Handler Flow:**
+```python:912-950:C7_GUI_D_WaveformWidget.py
+def _handle_dropped_files(self, file_paths):
+    # ... file loading logic ...
+    # Step 3: CRITICAL! Call finalize_file_load(True) to trigger BPM/Key analysis
+    app_controller.file_state_manager.finalize_file_load(True)
+```
+
+**Analysis Triggering:**
+```python:222-229:C7_GUI_Z_StateManagers.py
+def finalize_file_load(self, load_success: bool):
+    if load_success:
+        if self.current_file_path and self.async_manager:
+            self.logger.info(f"[FileStateManager] Starting BPM/Key analysis for: {self.current_file_path}")
+            self.async_manager.start_analysis(self.current_file_path)
+```
+
+**Worker Validation:**
+```python:68-74:C7_GUI_Z_AsyncManager.py
+def start_analysis(self, file_path: str):
+    if not self.bpm_key_thread or not self.bpm_key_worker:
+        error_msg = "BPM/Key worker is not set up. Call setup_bpm_key_worker() first."
+        self.logger.error(f"[AsyncManager] {error_msg}")
+        self.analysis_error.emit(error_msg)
+        return
+```
+
+## Impact Analysis
+
+### **What Works:**
+- Waveform loading (handled by `AudioEngine` directly)
+- UI responsiveness during file loading
+- First song analysis and UI updates
+
+### **What's Broken:**
+- Second+ song BPM analysis (worker destroyed)
+- Second+ song Key analysis (worker destroyed) 
+- Title field updates (depends on successful analysis completion flow)
+- UI consistency (shows old data for new song)
+
+### **Why Title Updates Fail:**
+The title update likely depends on the successful completion of the analysis workflow. When analysis fails due to missing worker, the complete UI update sequence is interrupted.
+
+## Solutions Architecture
+
+### **Option 1: Persistent Worker (Recommended)**
+- Modify `AsyncManager` to reuse workers instead of destroying them
+- Only destroy worker on app shutdown, not after each analysis
+- Cleaner resource management, better performance
+
+### **Option 2: Auto-Recreate Worker**  
+- Modify `start_analysis()` to call `setup_bpm_key_worker()` if worker is missing
+- Requires storing the analysis functions in AsyncManager
+- More overhead but maintains current cleanup pattern
+
+### **Option 3: Proper Cleanup References**
+- Fix the variable name bugs in `_handle_thread_finished()`
+- Ensure workers are properly cleaned up without breaking future analyses
+- Minimal change but requires careful thread management
+
+## Code Sections Requiring Changes
+
+1. **`C7_GUI_Z_AsyncManager.py`** - Primary fix location
+   - `_handle_thread_finished()` method
+   - Worker lifecycle management  
+   - Possibly `start_analysis()` method
+
+2. **`C7_GUI_Z_StateManagers.py`** - May need error handling improvements
+   - `FileStateManager.finalize_file_load()` 
+   - Better fallback when analysis fails
+
+3. **`C7_GUI_1_AppController.py`** - May need signal connection updates  
+   - Depending on chosen solution approach
+
+## Testing Strategy
+
+1. **Reproduction Test:** Load Song 1 ‚Üí Load Song 2 ‚Üí Verify all UI fields update
+2. **Worker Lifecycle Test:** Verify worker persists or recreates properly  
+3. **Multiple Song Test:** Load 3+ songs in succession
+4. **Error Recovery Test:** Simulate analysis failures and recovery
+5. **Resource Cleanup Test:** Verify no memory leaks from worker management
+
+---
+**Next Step:** Implement Option 1 (Persistent Worker) as it provides the cleanest solution with best performance characteristics.
+
+

-# Dist Build Startup Failure on M1 Max (Sonoma 14.5): Research & Analysis
-
-## Restated Feature/Problem
-A user attempted to run the distributed (dist) build of Qie on a MacBook Pro (M1 Max, macOS Sonoma 14.5). After moving Qie to Applications and double-clicking, the app icon appeared in the dock but the app never opened. Running the executable directly via terminal produced a Python traceback (see below). No logs were generated in `~/Library/Logs/Qie`, suggesting the app did not reach its own startup logic.
-
-**Terminal Output:**
-```
-/Applications/Qie.app/Contents/MacOS/Qie ; exit;
-andrew@Andrews-MBP ~ % /Applications/Qie.app/Contents/MacOS/Qie ; exit;
-Traceback (most recent call last):
-  File "PyInstaller/hooks/rthooks/pyi_rth_pkgres.py", line 177, in <module>
-  File "PyInstaller/hooks/rthooks/pyi_rth_pkgres.py", line 44, in _pyi_rthook
-  File "PyInstaller/loader/pyimod02_importers.py", line 457, in exec_module
-  File "pkg_resources/__init__.py", line 42, in <module>
-  File "PyInst
-```
-_(truncated)_
-
-## Inferences from the Traceback
-- The error occurs **very early** in the app startup, before any of our own code or logging is reached.
-- The traceback references `PyInstaller` runtime hooks, specifically `pyi_rth_pkgres.py` and `pkg_resources`.
-- The error is likely related to the PyInstaller bootloader or a missing/corrupted dependency in the bundled environment.
-- The truncated traceback prevents seeing the exact exception, but common issues at this stage include:
-  - Incompatible or missing Python packages (especially `pkg_resources`/`setuptools`)
-  - Architecture mismatch (e.g., x86_64 vs arm64)
-  - PyInstaller not bundling all required files for M1 Macs
-  - Code signing or macOS security restrictions (less likely if the error is in Python, not a system dialog)
-
-## Why No Logs?
-- Our runtime logs (e.g., `~/Library/Logs/Qie`) are only created after our Python entrypoint runs. If the app fails in the PyInstaller bootloader or before our code executes, **no logs will be generated**.
-
-## Steps to Improve Developer Diagnostics for Remote Users
-
-### 1. **Improve Error Visibility**
-- **Bundle a shell script** (e.g., `Qie_Debug.sh`) in the dist that:
-  - Runs the app from terminal
-  - Captures stdout/stderr to a file (e.g., `~/Desktop/Qie_debug_output.txt`)
-  - Instructs the user to send this file back
-- **Add a README** in the `.dmg` or `.zip` with troubleshooting steps:
-  - How to run the app from terminal
-  - Where to find/copy logs
-  - How to check for security blocks (System Settings > Privacy & Security)
-
-### 2. **PyInstaller Boot Diagnostics**
-- Enable PyInstaller's `--debug` flags during build (e.g., `--debug=all`) to get more verbose output in the terminal.
-- Consider building a special "diagnostic" version with extra logging or a minimal entrypoint that just prints environment info.
-
-### 3. **Architecture & Dependency Checks**
-- Ensure the build is universal or arm64-native for M1/M2 Macs.
-- Double-check that all dependencies (especially `setuptools`, `pkg_resources`) are bundled and compatible.
-- Test the build on a clean M1 Mac VM or with a tool like [`macOS VM`](https://github.com/sickcodes/Docker-OSX).
-
-### 4. **User-Friendly Crash Reporting**
-- If possible, add a top-level `try/except` in the entrypoint to catch and log any exceptions to a file on the Desktop or Documents folder, even if our main logic hasn't started.
-- Consider using a minimal C or shell wrapper that always logs stdout/stderr to a file.
-
-### 5. **Collect System Info**
-- Provide a script or instructions for users to run `system_profiler SPSoftwareDataType SPHardwareDataType` and `uname -a` to capture OS and hardware info.
-
-## Next Steps
-- **Do not apply code changes yet.**
-- Review PyInstaller build logs for missing modules or warnings.
-- Prepare a diagnostic build or script for remote users.
-- Update documentation to include user troubleshooting steps for dist builds.
-
----
-**References:**
-- [PyInstaller Troubleshooting](https://pyinstaller.org/en/stable/usage.html#troubleshooting)
-- [Apple Silicon (M1/M2) PyInstaller Issues](https://github.com/pyinstaller/pyinstaller/issues/5664)
-- [macOS Gatekeeper and App Not Opening](https://support.apple.com/en-us/HT202491)
